Current Situation of China-West Pharmacy 123

The other day, the China-West Pharmacy held a board meeting at Gongdelin, and all directors, including Chairman Chu Minyi, attended. The meeting items included the establishment of a broadcasting radio station, the addition of pill-making machines, the expansion of the machine manufacturing department, the preparation of injectable drugs and medical equipment, and the organization of a product review committee. It is also heard that the company's industrial department license has also been obtained. The 20th year's dividend was started to be issued on May 1st. Among the old brand star cosmetics issued by the pharmacy, the Star Flower Dew Perfume has the widest sales volume. Recently, large and small towns and cities in all provinces of the country have sent letters requesting to be distributors.

Saturday Weekly Published Today 124

Saturday Weekly, which has always been known for its humor and excellence, has been in publication for nine years. Today, at the beginning of its tenth year, it is being issued bound into a volume. The content has been increased by two times, and there are many sharp criticisms. Political, economic, and social issues are all written by experts. Literary and artistic content includes masterpieces by Du He, Shou Juan, Henshui, Zhuo Dai, Zhong Xian, Ding Song, and Ban Kuang, which are extremely lovely. It is said that all newspaper sellers in this city have it for sale. The annual subscription price will not be increased temporarily and remains at one yuan. The distribution department is at No. 311 Shandong Road.

The Lack of Momentum Causes Prices to Waver 131

Market Overview: Currently, the price of foreign silk (洋厘) ought to be high due to seasonal demand and ample supply opportunities. However, the devastation after the war has prevented recovery, causing a missed opportunity. In terms of the current situation, Chinese merchants have very little capacity to compete in the silkworm cocoon market. Recently, only foreign firms have made some preparations to export foreign silk. It is feared that there are few silkworm rearers in the mainland, resulting in limited production. Therefore, the price of foreign silk, despite attempts to rise, is consistently suppressed, resulting in prices remaining in flux.

Price Fluctuations: The morning market for "foreign silk" was quite lively due to bank purchases, and the price increased by 1.5 cents (厘) from the previous afternoon, reaching 7 qian (錢) and 5 cents. The afternoon trend weakened, and the closing price fell by a small 3 hao (毫) and 7 hu (忽) and a half from the morning, settling at 7 qian, 4 cents, 6 hao, and 2.5 hu. "Silver Sycee Exchange" (銀拆) was 4 fen (分) for both the morning and afternoon markets, seemingly better than the previous day by 2 fen. Adding a premium for clipped silver and water content was also common, with rates of 7-8 fen. This slightly improved situation, after a long period of relaxed credit conditions, is likely difficult to sustain.

Silver and Foreign Currency Inflow and Outflow: "Silver Funds" (銀欵) received by banks were significantly lower compared to the days before the market closure. Foreign banks received over 3.1 million in drafts, while Chinese banks received over 2.1 million. Goods receipts amounted to 3.2-3.3 million, and remittance receipts were 1.3-1.4 million. Foreign banks had over 600,000 in mortgage loans, while Chinese banks had only 300,000. Additionally, over 4 million was received in special funds, foreign currency, and miscellaneous funds. Foreign firms deposited 700,000 into warehouses, while Chinese firms withdrew 1 million. Money shops and silver firms received over 26.6 million in receipts, silver clipping premium receipts were over 4.22 million, inter-regional remittances were over 900,000, and cash receipts were 7-800,000. "Foreign Currency" (洋欵) remittance drafts were made at 610,000 in the morning market and 411,000 in the afternoon market. Banknotes were 55,000 in the morning and 40,000 in the afternoon. Furthermore, off-market banknotes were transacted at 105,000 in the afternoon market. Check transactions were 75,000 in the morning and 60,000 in the afternoon. Bank inflows and outflows were 500,000 in the morning and 400,000 in the afternoon. Bank transactions with foreign clients amounted to over 2.1 million, and banknote receipts and disbursements were over 2 million. Money shops received over 6.2-6.3 million in foreign currency, and foreign currency premium receipts were 1.8-1.9 million. Interbank lending of foreign currency was 1.6-1.7 million, inflows from the Yangtze River region were over 500,000, mainland freight was over 300,000, and small money shop transactions were over 600,000.

Subsidiary Coin Market: Early in the morning, Jiangnan small silver coins were bought by cocoon merchants, causing the price to rise by 4 cents, reaching 6 qian, 1 fen, and 9 cents. Afternoon trading was quiet, so the price did not move. Transactions totaled 7,500 jiao (角) in the morning and 3,000 jiao in the afternoon. Early in the morning, Guangdong small silver coins were 6 qian, 3 cents, and 7.5 hao, and in the afternoon, they were 6 qian, 3 cents, and 3.75 hao. Overall, they seemed to have risen by about 2 cents compared to the previous afternoon. Transactions totaled 115,000 jiao in the morning and 15,000 jiao in the afternoon. Copper coins were slightly short by 500 wen (文), estimated at 415,000,000 wen.

A Glimpse of Silver, Foreign Currency, and Goods Activity in the Last Two Days 132

Over the past two days, foreign banks on the Bund have expanded their business operations as the market closure period had passed. With the Shanghai settlement signed, people's hearts have been greatly reassured. Letters and telegrams for purchasing goods from various ports have been exchanged frequently, and telegraphic and mail remittances have also arrived in a continuous stream. Foreign merchants have received no less than 1 million in electronic transfers, while Chinese merchants have also received 5-600,000. Consequently, the export of goods has also flourished, especially the import of foreign goods, which has been significant, leading to substantial customs revenue. Yesterday's customs revenue was as high as 6-700,000. The vigorous flow of goods has naturally created a need for silver and foreign currency, but the ample reserves have prevented the market from being significantly affected.

Yarn Market Falls for Three Consecutive Days 134

Possibility of a Turnaround

The cotton yarn market is showing signs of improvement. After falling for three consecutive days, dropping significantly by 4-5 liang (兩) from the opening price, some profiteers seized the opportunity to buy short, causing the market sentiment to rebound slightly. In addition, with the signing of the Sino-Japanese armistice agreement, market sentiment suddenly tightened, leading to a shortage of sellers in the market. As a result, the market situation suddenly became firm. However, there is still no overly optimistic expectation for the overall trend, as the inventory of various factories in the market is too large, the Northeast war is fierce, and credit conditions cannot be fully revitalized. How can commerce turn around? However, the tendered yarn price is already 6-7 liang cheaper than the current yarn market price, but outsiders, considering the still deteriorating environment, have not abandoned the idea of shorting.

Man-Tender Scattered Shorts Covered: In the morning opening of Man-Tender (人標), the market sentiment was better due to the rise in American cotton and good news about the situation. The situation was slightly tight, with more buyers. Scattered shorts covered, with various months rising by 8-9 qian to 1 liang. In the afternoon, it was heard that actual demand was not smooth, and the market situation turned weak again. Near-month contracts fell by 3.1 qian, and far-month contracts rose by 1.4 qian. The total trading volume for the day was 6,300 bales. Among them, Hengyi sold 350 bales, Changfeng sold 350 bales, Dachang sold 400 bales, Jifeng sold 150 bales, Taichang sold 400 bales, and Yichang sold 250 bales. Silk and Tea: New York Cantonese Silk Prices Plunge 141

Fine Silk Opens at $1.06, Coarse Silk at $0.82

Due to the repeated and drastic falls in Japanese silk prices, the New York raw silk market was affected, and Chinese silk followed a weak trend. Cantonese silk prices are based on Japanese silk and its fluctuations, so the degree of the price drop was even greater. Fine filaments opened at only $1.06 per pound, and coarse filaments opened at $0.82, each falling by 6-7 jiao from the highest price.

Foreign Firms' Silk Market Continues to Be Sluggish 142

The local foreign firms' silk market is lifeless. Although there are overseas silk telegrams forwarding to Shanghai, the incoming prices are still low. Chinese silk merchants' losses are too great, making it difficult to sell. The market sentiment continues to stagnate.

Qimen Baihao Price Reaches Its Peak 143

Due to the tender tea buds that have been harvested in Qimen these past few days, shipments have not been abundant. Moreover, due to the cold and rainy weather these past couple days, tea buds are developing slowly. Due to the lack of sunshine, it is not advantageous to dry the tea, so most families have stopped picking tea, waiting for the weather to clear up and get warmer so tea buds can grow longer and continue to be harvested and processed. Because new tea has not officially entered the market, only 60-70% of the tea estates have started their harvest. In addition, it is difficult to transport the tea via the river transport to the port for export to foreign lands. Most firms are experiencing the difficulty of having goods but not enough money to procure them. Currently, most firms are preparing to procure money from the Qiupu region to purchase tea; however, this is just a drop in the bucket. Merchants that operate in Qiupu demand a high price for each thousand liang, raising the price to 1,300 yuan, which is a difference of 100 yuan in comparison to Jingdezhen/Tunxi. Tea firms are knowingly taking a loss but are helpless against the circumstances. Recently, a new harvest from Jiangjia river in Qimen was once bid at 110-120 yuan, but quickly fell to 80 yuan due to a lack of funds. The market price for raw Baihao is 230 yuan. The finished Gong tea would cost 400 yuan which is around 60-70 liang higher than last year. With the price reaching its peak, the current raw prices are unprecedented.

Wuyuan Tea Firms Decreases by More Than 20 Firms 144

Wuyuan tea firms used to have over 300 farms in the whole town. With the northeast and two towns taking up the majority. This year, various firms have predicted the chaos stemming from nearby rebellions, difficulties in the river transport, and tight funds. Due to these difficulties, the firms are pessimistic towards the tea business. Recently, stock from factories in Shanghai has been sold, and foreign firms are in high demand, the tea production is important for the town and local farmers. The firms are forced to enter the market. By the latest count, aside from the new firms established in the towns of Zhangchun Jixianglong and Sikou Yitaixiang and 3-4 factories that have moved to the northeast side, the number of firms has stayed the same in the west. In the south side,玉坦·太白·中雲 and other tea firms are nearby the rebel areas, with 20 firms fully shut down with no opening. There are a few firms planning to move to the northeast to operate. In total, 20 firms from the 4 towns have decreased.

2,000 Bags Offered in the Morning Market

Yesterday, the sugar market at the Sugar Association was active. Dutch No. 24 coarse sand and white sugar traded at 12 liang and 8 qian and 5 fen. High-quality goods were priced at 12 liang and 9 qian. Hong Kong goods were priced at 12 liang, 6 qian, 8 fen, 7.5 li to 12 liang and 7 qian. Supply was particularly scarce, and the market was very active. No. 20 medium sand and white was priced at 12 liang and 5 qian and 5 fen, and No. 8 Dutch red was priced at 9 liang and 5 qian and 5 fen, slightly higher at 9 liang and 6 qian and 5 fen, with an upward trend. Important News

Jiangsu Education Department Temporarily Dissolves Xuzhou Senior High School Students 147

Key Instigators to Be Detained for Investigation and Handling

Senior Normal School Grade 3 to Be Expelled; Junior High Resumes Classes

Since Xue Zhongtai took over as principal of Jiangsu Provincial Xuzhou High School, his management has been quite serious. Recently, students in the Senior Normal School Grade 3 class requested that the school subsidize their field trip expenses. Xue submitted a report to the Education Department, stating that due to the national crisis and traffic disruptions in the province, many schools in the Beijing-Shanghai area have not been proceeding as usual. All field trips for this year's schools should be suspended. However, the students still requested to go to Shandong and Beiping, demanding even higher fees. Xue, unable to disobey the Education Department's order and facing severe financial difficulties, repeatedly tried to reason with the students, but they ignored him. The students in the class initially threatened to suspend their studies as a whole, then incited all high school students to occupy the two campuses, expel faculty and staff, and force the principal to leave. They also submitted a petition to the Education Department in the name of all students, attacking the principal. The Education Department deemed that the students' unreasonable coercion and incitement of a strike were extreme actions beyond the pale, so it not only issued a stern rebuke to the students but also telegraphed the Jinpu Garrison Command and the Tongshan County Chief to assist in strict handling. It also ordered the Provincial Supervisor Yi Zuolin to go to the school, detain the key instigators for investigation and handling, and expel all students involved in the turmoil in that class. Their security deposits will be deducted, and they will be required to repay all food and lodging expenses. The other high school students who supported the trouble-making, causing the turmoil to escalate, should be temporarily dissolved as a whole. As for the junior high students, they were ordered to resume classes immediately. According to the Education Department, it will spare no sacrifices and overcome any difficulties to investigate and handle the matter strictly to thoroughly rectify the situation and reverse the uproar.

Jiangsu Provincial Xuzhou People's Education Center Opens 148

Since the Education Department appointed Zhao Guangtao as the preparatory director to start preparations for the Jiangsu Provincial Xuzhou People's Education Center, progress has been quite rapid. Last year, the Education Department sent Section Chief Yu Qingting to Xuzhou to survey the site, which was located between the northeast two stations, purchasing 21 mu (畝) of land for 3,500 yuan. After three months of active preparation, and with the Education Department appointing Zhao Guangtao as the director, the official opening ceremony was held on May 1st. As the new site is still under construction, the ceremony was temporarily held at the preparatory office. The ceremony was simple, and representatives from various agencies and organizations attended, as well as township chiefs. During this time of national crisis and disaster, it is fortunate to witness this educational construction. According to investigations, the center has now established two experimental zones in the Bajie and Xiadian areas of the suburbs. The people's school has opened three classes, with a total of 150 students. Two reading rooms have been established, and ten bulletin boards have been set up. A credit cooperative has been established, as well as two joint farmers' loan associations. 10,000 trees have been planted on barren hills. The social surveys, agricultural surveys, and industrial surveys of the experimental zones have also been completed and are being compiled. Specially contracted people's tea gardens and industrial training classes are also being prepared and established. An anti-Japanese exhibition and an agricultural exhibition are being prepared, as well as a village citizen improvement association in the experimental zone, etc., which can be expected to be completed soon. It is heard that the center focuses on rural people's education, aiming for the balanced development of intelligence among urban and rural people, not limited to urban people's education.

Local News

Shanghai Municipal Council Subsidy for Chinese Private Schools in the Concession Must Be Approved by the Municipal Education Bureau 149

Yesterday, an education reporter, concerned about reports that the Shanghai Municipal Council's subsidy for Chinese private schools in the concession seemed to be related to Chinese educational rights, interviewed an important official of the Municipal Education Bureau for inquiries. The following is a record of the conversation: The Shanghai Municipal Council previously planned to subsidize Chinese private schools in the concession and sought the consent of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau. The Municipal Education Bureau submitted its compiled opinions to the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government for instructions. It then sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council, requesting them to follow the instructions, but has not yet received a reply and cannot implement it immediately. According to the previous results of the Education Bureau's decision with the Municipal Council, Chinese schools established in the concession, if they have been registered or approved by the Education Bureau for trial operation, must first submit an application to the Education Bureau for approval before the Education Bureau can forward it to the Municipal Council for consent in order to obtain the Municipal Council's subsidy. However, yesterday (the 6th), various newspapers suddenly published two articles on the Municipal Council's subsidy for Chinese private schools in the concession, with a statement that "schools that have not been registered can directly apply to the Superintendent of Education at the Municipal Council and obtain a blank application form for completion." The Education Bureau believes that subsidizing private schools that have not been approved for registration or trial operation violates the Ministry's regulations for private schools. This record is quite misleading. It is heard that the Education Bureau will wait for the Municipal Council's reply and completion of the procedures before notifying all private schools in the Public Concession to implement the measure. In addition to the Municipal Council's proposed subsidy for private schools, the Education Bureau also has procedures for applying for subsidy fees approved by the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government, which will be notified to all schools at that time. It is hoped that the schools will not be misled by yesterday's news.

Establishment of the Shanghai Secondary School Disaster Relief Committee 150

The Shanghai Secondary School Disaster Relief Committee held its first inaugural meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday inside the Nanyang High School of Commerce on Weihaiwei Road. Representatives present included Wu Jiangleng (Nanyang), Lao Jianshao (Zhizhi Affiliated Middle School), Wang Zhongming (Xinmin), Hu Zigan (Minsheng), Jiang Jingkai (Anzhong), Sun Xiangzhong (Aiguo), Senior Qiu (China Women's Physical Education), Jiang Yancheng (Guangong), Chen Yun, Sheng (Daozhong). The proceedings were conducted formally. Chairman Wu Jiangleng declared that various universities were already preparing for a disaster relief committee, and that the losses suffered by secondary schools were no less than those of the universities, making an organization necessary. After deliberation, it was decided to divide the committee into four sections: Documentation, Accounting, Public Relations, and General Affairs. Key resolutions were as follows: (A) The committee staff will primarily consist of representatives from affected schools, allocated based on the number of students affected. (B) Standing members will be organized into teams, each responsible for specific duties. (C) Public relations will be handled by representatives from the affected schools. (D) Cadres will be organized into teams. (E) A survey will be conducted to determine the exact number of affected schools. (F) The committee will treat all affected schools equally, regardless of whether they are officially registered, without discrimination. (G) The committee's primary objective is to seek compensation for losses from the government, with all matters to be handled by the government, regardless of whether the schools are officially registered. (H) For the election of committee members, each school present will initially nominate twelve individuals, with the remaining members to be added later. (I) The committee will meet every two weeks, with a quorum of more than half of the members. (J) The committee's address will temporarily be within the Nanyang High School of Commerce on Weihaiwei Road. All the above resolutions were unanimously passed, and the meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM.

Free Talk

Signing Before the Bed 156

— Song Lu

The peace conference has concluded. The ceasefire agreement has been transcribed and sent to the representatives of both sides to sign "before the bed." Patriotic groups are constantly shouting their opposition. However, the general public, who deeply love peace, are undoubtedly offering "sincere prayers" there.

The most interesting thing is the phrase "before the bed." Tang poetry says, "Moonlight before the bed, I suspect it is frost on the ground. I raise my head to gaze at the bright moon, I lower my head and think of my hometown." Now, I wonder if our representatives, when signing before the bed, thought of this Tang poem and then thought of our "hometown." What thoughts did they have in their hearts?

The Zuo Zhuan says, "Words spoken in the bedroom shall not cross the threshold." Because words spoken in the bedroom should only be spoken in bed, they must be kept absolutely secret. Now, this "peace conference" has always been held in "secrecy" from beginning to end. Because it is secret, the signing must also be done in bed.

The representatives of China and Japan are both signing in bed because they are injured. I think it would be good to place the two beds side by side and have a "night talk in connected beds, with feet touching." Unfortunately, both Ambassador Chongguang and Lieutenant General Ueda have injured feet. It would be a little inconvenient to touch "feet."

As I wrote this, a pedantic Mr. Er saw it and said, "No wonder the two governments have always talked about 'Sino-Japanese friendship.' It turns out that the two are really very good together. As the saying goes, 'Don't try to stop a couple from fighting. Just need a bed...' Now, China and Japan have been fighting for months. Sure enough, they just did this on the 'bed,' and then they got better again." I couldn't help but laugh when I heard this. Oh, so that's how it is.

Free Aphorisms 157

— Yu Xiang

An Englishman's love of freedom is like his legally wedded wife, whose wedding was held in a church and formally officiated by a pastor. She entirely, is something that belongs to him. Perhaps because home flowers are not as fragrant as wild flowers, he may not treat her very tenderly. However, he will never relax his reasonable and adequate protection of her and is very willing to be responsible for her to the end.

In the eyes of a Frenchman, freedom is simply as lovely as the lover he privately loves. To take the analogy a step further, a Frenchman views freedom like a pretty and moving wild rose. It has brilliant colors, it also has a rich fragrance, and it has a sweet taste. But ah, it is covered with sharp thorns. If you are not careful, it may break the skin. However, a lecherous Frenchman, for the sake of freedom, will go through fire and water, and sacrifice himself, no matter what the sacrifice. Indeed, he is obsessed with freedom.

Let's talk about a German. His attitude toward freedom is exactly like treating his old grandmother. That is to say, he only respects it solemnly and does not love it passionately.

Although that's how it is said, who can predict the changes in the world?

When an Englishman gets angry, he may harden his heart and give his wife a beating or a scolding, deeply trampling on her.

The Frenchman, then, is even more dangerous. The weeds and wildflowers in the alleys and streets exert an irresistible attraction, making it possible for him to abandon his lover at any time. Indeed, in France, finding a new lover is not a difficult thing.

But the German will never have this kind of bad temper or do this kind of ungrateful thing. He will not be very cold to his old grandmother. He wants his beloved and respected old grandmother to always rest on the sofa in the living room. There, she can tell some fairy tales to her grandchildren.

Zuo Maodi 159

— Gu Mingdao

When the League of Nations investigation team went to the three northeastern provinces, our country sent Mr. Gu Weijun as a representative to accompany them. It was right and proper. However, Japan instigated the puppet state to repeatedly and firmly reject this. Their opposition to China and disregard for the League of Nations is clearly visible. He was detained in the north. Upon hearing of the fall of Jiangnan, he did not eat for seven days. The Qing regent summoned him. Maodi, wearing mourning clothes, a filial cap, and straw sandals, bowed deeply to the regent, sitting facing south. Maodi argued, only asking for death. He refused to shave his head. He was killed on June 19. He wrote a poem before his death: "The gorge is split, the nest is sealed, the return path is far. The traveling clouds go south, what is the intention? The inch of red heart and cold spirit cannot be exhausted, it will turn into smoke and clouds and will not be ground down." His followers Chen Yongji and Wang Yibin and others all died for their principles. Although Zuo Maodi was a scholar, he was able to face death calmly, without humiliation to the barbarian. As the saying goes, "A scholar can be killed, but not humiliated." His high moral integrity is admirable. I wonder if Mr. Gu today can also encourage himself in this way.

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter Six: Pitifully, They Were Forced into a Bedside Alliance on the Night of a Shared Dream, Still Recalling the First Love When They Broke the Window Pact

Liang Xiaoyun said loudly, "That won't do. Can this kind of relationship be casually talked about with a laugh? If I say it too shallowly, people will suspect I'm just meddling. They might not agree. If I say it more deeply, then, according to this situation, what exactly are the two of us? Mom vaguely told people like that. I would lose too much face." An Yutian was secretly shocked. Of course, he had already heard the meaning in her words, but he thought the relationship was too important, so he didn't want to make an obvious expression first. She said, "Of course, there is a very appropriate way to say it, but that is a matter of proper status and cannot be casually said as a joke. Even this time, when we start drilling into the door to see Governor Ye, as soon as I mention that I have married you, such a young husband, they will have to pay special attention."

Science

Sugar 163

— Tao Xiaotao

Sugar is something that we cannot live without in our lives. The reason why our human body generates body temperature is because of carbohydrates and fats (carbohydrates are the general term for starch and sugar). Carbohydrates combine with oxygen in the body and give us the ability to perform various tasks. Each of us normally needs 13 and a half taels of carbohydrates every day to have enough strength to work.

There are three types of raw materials for sugar production: sugarcane, beet, and maple tree. The places in the world that produce cane sugar are Cuba, Guangdong and Fujian in our country. The places that produce beet sugar are Germany and France, and the places that produce maple sugar are Canada and the United States. Our country does not produce beet sugar or maple sugar, only a small amount of cane sugar is produced. Now, because the space is very short, the production of beet and maple sugar, etc., will be discussed later, only cane sugar production will be discussed. According to Tiangong Kaiwu, our country did not know how to produce sugar before. It was not until the Dali period of the Tang Dynasty (1146 years before the Republic of China) that a Western monk Zou traveled to Suining County, Sichuan, and began to spread the method of planting sugarcane and making sugar. The current method of making sugar is to first press the sugarcane juice out, then filter it with lime milk, and put the clarified sugar liquid in a vacuum pot to cook. Why put it in a vacuum pot to cook? When we boil water on the high mountains, the water boils when it reaches 80-90 degrees Celsius, because the air is thin on the high mountains and the pressure is low. Cooking in a vacuum pot can save time and coal. Therefore, a vacuum pot is used to evaporate. After evaporation, wait for it to cool and crystallize into raw sugar. This raw sugar is dissolved, filtered with bone ash, and then put into a vacuum pot to cook. After cooling, it becomes pure white sugar.

Our country's recent annual production of sugar is 200,000 tons, and consumption is 1,000,000 tons.

Medicine

Prescription 164

— Zi Dong

Hua'er's illness has reached a very dangerous period. The parents in Washington are so worried that they have invited many famous doctors to their home to treat him.

After taking the pulse and measuring the temperature, many doctors gathered together to discuss the method of treatment.

A said, "The patient's body is too weak. It is best to take more tonic medicines, such as ginseng, deer antler, ... the more the better. This is a 'comprehensive plan' method."

B said, "No, the reason for his illness is due to feeling external evil. Tonic medicines are completely inappropriate. It is better to use some releasing agents to implement a military expulsion of the disease demon."

C said, "The patient's temperature is very high. Hurry up and get some ice to cool him down and lower his temperature."

D said, "I think it is better to give him a few blood-replenishing injections to maintain his sick body so that he can resist the disease demon for a long time."

E said, "..."

You say a sentence, he says a sound, and gradually, from a gentle discussion, it turns into a fierce debate. Finally, they roll up their sleeves and fight with each other. After the parents in Washington persuaded them to leave, they sent them out one by one.

Hua'er sighed in bed, "If I don't take their prescriptions, I can still linger on. If I take their prescriptions, I am sure to lose my life immediately."

Day after day passed, and Hua'er's illness became more and more serious. Every day, several baskets of prescriptions were thrown out of the Washington mansion, which benefited Zhang Laoer, who sold groceries, who used them to wrap copper coins, wrap peanuts, and wrap everything.

A Corner of Society

Shanghai Sketches, No. 2 165

— I

丨丨The Crowd of Applicants

The Gu residence's messenger was now being summoned to the second young master's study. Usually, it wasn't easy for him to go to the young masters' rooms, but today was an exception. At the door, the large foreign parrot greeted him with a "Hello." As he entered, he heard a burst of the maid's laughter, after which he saw the maid coyly hiding towards the back room.

A wisp of smoke swirled in the green light reflected from the green leaves outside the window, and the blood-red roses in front of the steps boldly sent in their rich fragrance, along with the smiling face of the girl on the wall; everything deepened the richness of spring. He thought,

"Ah! The young master is truly blessed!"

At this moment, the second young master was fixing his tie in front of the dressing mirror, then applying a little Stanco pomade, so his black hair shone with a dark luster. Afterwards, the young master noticed the messenger waiting for his orders, so he solemnly said:

"There will be quite a few women coming today. Bring the pretty and young ones to see me. If too many come, just bring one in every half hour. Tell the rest to come back tomorrow."

"Yes, young master! I understand."

In fact, the messenger was completely baffled. However, since he had received the young master's order, he had to execute it carefully; there was nothing to say. Fortunately, he saw the maid who usually served the second young master walking in from outside in the courtyard. So, with a smile, he inquired, and learned that the second young master had placed an advertisement in the newspaper yesterday, seeking a female secretary. As for the young master saying he wanted someone "young and pretty," he knew what this female secretary would be used for.

"Humph! The young master really knows how to have fun."

When he returned to the door, he saw a female student in a skirt already waiting for him. He thought, "That was fast! Business has arrived." But although this first one was young, she wasn't very pretty. However, since this was the first of the day, he would take her in once.

"Are you here to apply for the secretary position?" the messenger asked.

"Yes!" The girl blushed.

"Then go see the young master."

When the messenger returned the second time, there were two more waiting at the door. Soon another came in. This was really bad. Three had come all at once, which one should he take in first? And there was still one inside who hadn't come out.

"I think you should come back tomorrow afternoon. Our young master hasn't gotten up yet."

"Ah?" One by one, they had to dejectedly turn away.

But then young and pretty ones came along. Then filled with tears, they went back. Only those who happened to be at the door just as the young master released one, and immediately filled the spot, could meet the young master; they were truly extremely lucky. Afterwards, applicants continued to come and continued to leave. Those in skirts, those in qipaos, and those in high-heeled leather shoes. Young ones, pretty ones. Until the evening, there were at least over twenty.

The first day was like this, the second day was like this, and the third day was still like this. He thought, "I wonder whose luck is good enough to get a job here." But a week later, he heard the maid in the second young master's room say:

"The young master is really having fun, women keep him company all day long; he's thinking of doing it again next month!"

Reasonable

Taking Advantage of the Disaster 166

— Tao Ge

Since the January 28th Shanghai Incident, all businesses have been at a standstill, especially those in the war zone, which have suffered heavy losses. As a result, many have declared bankruptcy and are being liquidated. However, there are also some who take advantage of this opportunity to deliberately dissolve their businesses, blaming it on the war, in order to seize unexpected profits.

A friend of mine had ordered a suit from the ×× Tailor Shop on North Sichuan Road before the war broke out. When the time came to pick it up, after paying in full, he discovered some discrepancies and asked them to modify it. Unexpectedly, the incident occurred that night, and he was unable to retrieve the suit for a long time. When the situation calmed down slightly, he went back to pick it up, but all the items in the store had been moved away. Only a notice was posted on the wall, roughly stating:

"Due to the great losses caused by the recent war, all goods have been looted, making it impossible to resume business. Therefore, we have no choice but to declare dissolution. We hope for your forgiveness."

The next day, an advertisement was published in the newspaper, saying: "Due to the Shanghai war, all items in the store were looted, resulting in heavy losses and making it impossible to resume business. Therefore, according to the resolution of the shareholders' meeting, we hereby announce the dissolution. All former colleagues are kindly requested to seek other employment and not to waste any more time and effort."

My friend sighed, thinking it was just bad luck, and decided not to pursue the matter. Unexpectedly, they ran into each other on Xiafei Road in the French Concession. He saw that the shop had reorganized and resumed business. The only difference was that the word "Branch" was added below the old name. My friend was very angry and went inside to question them. He found that not only was the counter the same as before, but all the staff had not changed either. After a long period of questioning, even banging on chairs and tables, the shop assistant led him upstairs, where he saw suits piled up like a mountain. In the end, he returned in triumph. Another friend had a similar experience with repairing a watch. Alas! Where is the conscience in "taking advantage of the disaster"?

Study

Student Life During National Crisis 167

— Meng Ping

After the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the Chinese schools in Zhabei all moved to the "safe area" to hold classes. The so-called safe area refers to the Shanghai concessions. It merely uses the protection of foreigners to prevent the schools from being affected by the war. This fact is very painful. Now I will talk about the lives of the students.

Most of the students live outside the school, because the school cannot rent many houses for students to live in. Life outside the school is very free. Not only do they not need to ask for leave to enter and exit, but their actions are also not restricted by the instructors. They can ask someone to attend class for them and play outside all day, and it doesn't matter. In the afternoon, they can stroll in the park for three or four hours, both to pursue the opposite sex and to relax their minds. At night, they play mahjong, saying it is to practice social skills, as a tool for serving society in the future. Gambling is very permissive in the safe area, and they will not be restricted by the outside world, so they gamble to their heart's content until dawn. Movie theaters and dance halls are places they frequent. They do not ask about national crises or imperialist aggression. Anyway, the country

doesn't belong to them personally.

What I have described above is certainly the life of some students. But this situation is increasingly expanding, like a contagious disease, spreading from a few people to many people. If they have not been vaccinated, it is very difficult to avoid it.

Editor's Note: Yesterday, we received a submission from Meng Ping entitled "Student Life During National Crisis." I do not know whether the life of students is really like this in some aspects. However, students are the masters of our country in the future, and the fate of the country depends entirely on the students. Therefore, publishing it here is also with the intention of correcting it if it is true, and encouraging it if it is not.

Nonsense

Short Talk 168

— Ren Jun

A and B were drinking together on the afternoon of May 5th.

A: Great, Shanghai won't have another war. The ceasefire agreement was signed yesterday.

B: Although the government has repeatedly stated that it will never sign treaties that betray our country and humiliate our nation, I'm still a bit skeptical.

A: Put your mind at ease! This is based on the resolution of the League of Nations, and it is also the government's so-called long-term resistance plan!

B: Hey! What long-term resistance? What final determination? Don't you see that the situation in the South is becoming urgent again?

A: You really don't understand. This is just practicing on our own, preparing to resist foreign aggression in the future!

B: Alas! In this vast land of China, I am grieving for the future!

A: Stop saying depressing things. Peace has been achieved. Let's have a drink to celebrate!

The two clinked glasses and drank, their hands slightly trembling, their eyes filled with tears, as if invaded by an inexplicable sorrow.
